http://fossldce.org/viewfull.php?index=15,nilesh dwivedi represented ldce at social innovations hackathon organized in rashtrapati bhavan

by ldce
                            / 19 mar, 2016

nilesh dwivedi students of be computer engineering has selected for code for india social innovations hackathon organized in rashtrapatibhavan on 19th march 2016 and represented l.d. college of engineering there. 
in this hackathon, closing keynote was given by the hon. president of india, shri pranab mukherjee.
during this he has made an android application named "loo-fi" that will solve the problem of surveillance of public loos. http: fossldce org viewfull php?index=15
